<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:защита.html>защи́та</a> (1412)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:защита.html>защи́та</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaščíta</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:защита.html>защи́ты</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:защита.html>защи́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:защита.html>защи́т</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>defense, protection, advocacy</li>
<li>aegis, shield, armour, shelter, cover
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">абляцио́нная <b><a href = vnd.unilang:защита.html>защи́та</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">abljaciónnaja <b>zaščíta</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ablative_armor" class="extiw" title="w:ablative armor">ablative armor</a></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>protection</li>
<li>defense, guard</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:защищать.html>защища́ть</a> (2527)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:защитить.html>защити́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zaščitítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:защищать.html>защища́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaščiščátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:защитить.html>защити́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to defend, to guard, to protect</li>
<li>to speak in support (of), to stand up for, to support, to vindicate, to advocate</li>
<li>to defend, to plead for <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in a court of law</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to uphold, to defend (a thesis, diploma or dissertation)</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:защищаться.html>защища́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaščiščátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:защититься.html>защити́ться</a></b>)

<ol><li>to defend oneself, to protect oneself</li>

<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:защищать.html>защища́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zaščiščátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:щи.html>щи</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ща́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:защититься.html>защити́ться</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-защища-</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

***заявить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заявить.html>заяви́ть</a> (1027)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:явить.html>яви́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">javítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заявить.html>заяви́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zajavítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заявлять.html>заявля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to declare, to announce</li>
<li>to say (of a high-rank person or ironically), to claim, to state</li>
<li>to apply <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to submit oneself as a candidate</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to file (a complaint to authorities or police)</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заявление.html>заявле́ние</a> (1631)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заявить.html>заяви́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zajavítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заявление.html>заявле́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zajavlénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заявление.html>заявле́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заявление.html>заявле́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заявление.html>заявле́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>declaration, statement</li>
<li>petition, application</li></ol>

***заявлять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заявлять.html>заявля́ть</a> (4503)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заявить.html>заяви́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zajavítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заявлять.html>заявля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zajavljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заявить.html>заяви́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to declare, to announce</li>
<li>to say (of a high-rank person or ironically), to claim, to state</li>
<li>to apply <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to submit oneself as a candidate</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to file (a complaint to authorities or police)</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>яв<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ля́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***званый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:званый.html>зва́ный</a> (26475)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звать.html>зва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ányj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:званый.html>зва́ный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zványj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>invited
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:много.html>мно́го</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:званый.html>зва́ных</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:маленький.html>мало</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:избранный.html>и́збранных</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mnógo zványx, da malo ízbrannyx</i> ― <span class="e-translation">many are called, but few are chosen</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>with invited guests
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:званый.html>зва́ный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:обед.html>обе́д</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zványj</b> obéd</i> ― <span class="e-translation">formal dinner party; banquet</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:званый.html>зва́ный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вечер.html>ве́чер</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zványj</b> véčer</i> ― <span class="e-translation">evening party; guest night</span></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can we date this quote?)</span>,  Mao Zedong,  <cite>Quotations from Chairman Mao Tse-tung</cite>, Classes and Class Struggle, <a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Quotations_from_Chairman_Mao_Tse-tung/Classes_and_Class_Struggle" class="extiw" title="s:Quotations from Chairman Mao Tse-tung/Classes and Class Struggle">chapter 2</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:революция.html>револю́ция</a> - <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:званый.html>зва́ный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:обед.html>обе́д</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Revoljúcija - éto ne <b>zványj</b> obéd</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">A revolution is not a <b>dinner</b> party</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Short forms <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:званный.html>зван</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:званный.html>зва́на</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:званный.html>зва́но</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:званный.html>зва́ны</a></span> theoretically exist, but are usually avoided due to their similarity to short forms of the past passive participle of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звать.html>зва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>зва́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <i>зва́нее, зва́ней.</i>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-зв-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-а-н</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

***звать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:звать.html>зва́ть</a> (545)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">зъвати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zŭvati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*zъvati</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звать.html>зва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:позвать.html>позва́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to call
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:звать.html>зову́т</a></b> Пётр.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Menjá <b>zovút</b> Pjótr.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">My name is Pyotr.</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">They <b>call</b> me Pyotr.</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to invite</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:звать.html>зва́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 6°b/c.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-зв-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звезда.html>звезда́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zvezdá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звезда.html>звезды́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звезда.html>звёзды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звезда.html>звёзд</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">astronomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> star (celestial body)

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:звезда.html>звезда́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:первый.html>пе́рвой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:величина.html>величины́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zvezdá</b> pérvoj veličiný</i> ― <span class="e-translation">star of the first magnitude</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>star (celebrity)

<p><b>звез<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да́</a></b> (<span title="написание в дореформенной орфографии" style="border-bottom: 1px dotted; cursor: help">дореформ.</span> <span style="font-family: | Palatino Linotype | ">звѣзда</span>)

Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> знач. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:знаменитость.html>знамени́тость</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склоняться.html>склоня́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:образец.html>образцу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>существи́тельных</a> (<span title="в винительном падеже"><a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кого́</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a>?</span> — <i><a href = vnd.unilang:звезда.html>звезду́</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:звезда.html>звёзд</a></i>).
